   <script>
    function highlightNav($ele) {
            if (window.link) {
                var $tree = $ele.find('.tree')
                $.each($tree, function () {
                    var $this = $(this)
                    var flag = true
                    if ($this.attr('data-link') === window.link) {
                        $this.addClass('active')

                        if ($this.find('.tree-view').length) {
                            $this.addClass('js_hover')
                        }
                        flag = false
                    }
                    return flag
                })
            }

            if (window.sub_link) {
                var $tree_view = $ele.find('.tree-view')
                $.each($tree_view, function () {
                    var $this = $(this)
                    var $item = $this.find('li')
                    var outerFlag = true
                    $.each($item, function () {
                        var $this = $(this)
                        var innerFlag = true
                        if ($this.attr('data-sub-link') === window.sub_link) {
                            $this.addClass('active')
                            innerFlag = false
                            outerFlag = false
                        }
                        return innerFlag
                    })
                    return outerFlag
                })
            }
        }

        function getQueryString(name) {
            var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)", "i");
            var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
            if (r != null) {
                return decodeURIComponent(r[2]);
            }
            return null;
        }


        var $side_nav = $('#side_nav')
        var $side_nav_replace = $('#side_nav1')

        if(window.link || window.sub_link){
            highlightNav($side_nav)
            highlightNav($side_nav_replace)
        } else {
            var eb_str = getQueryString('eb')
            if(eb_str) {
                var highlightArray = ['top-line', 'quick-news', 'sole', 'special-topic', 'special-column', 'news-retail', 'news-cross', 'news-industry'];
                var is_find = false;
                for (var i = 0; i < highlightArray.length; i += 1) {
                    var reg = new RegExp(highlightArray[i] + '$', 'ig');
                    if (reg.test(eb_str)) {
                        is_find = true;
                        var _str = highlightArray[i];
                        if (/news/g.test(_str)) {
                            var _str_array = highlightArray[i].split('-');
                            window.link = _str_array[0];
                            window.sub_link = _str_array[1];
                        } else {
                            window.link = _str;
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if(!is_find) {
                    window.link = "news"
                }
            } else {
                window.link = "news"
            }

            highlightNav($side_nav)
            highlightNav($side_nav_replace)
        }
   </script>

     <script>
      function highlightNav($ele) {
            if (window.link) {
                var $tree = $ele.find('.tree')
                $.each($tree, function () {
                    var $this = $(this)
                    var flag = true
                    if ($this.attr('data-link') === window.link) {
                        $this.addClass('active')

                        if ($this.find('.tree-view').length) {
                            $this.addClass('js_hover')
                        }
                        flag = false
                    }
                    return flag
                })
            }

            if (window.sub_link) {
                var $tree_view = $ele.find('.tree-view')
                $.each($tree_view, function () {
                    var $this = $(this)
                    var $item = $this.find('li')
                    var outerFlag = true
                    $.each($item, function () {
                        var $this = $(this)
                        var innerFlag = true
                        if ($this.attr('data-sub-link') === window.sub_link) {
                            $this.addClass('active')
                            innerFlag = false
                            outerFlag = false
                        }
                        return innerFlag
                    })
                    return outerFlag
                })
            }
        }

        function getQueryString(name) {
            var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)", "i");
            var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
            if (r != null) {
                return decodeURIComponent(r[2]);
            }
            return null;
        }


        var $side_nav = $('#side_nav')
        var $side_nav_replace = $('#side_nav1')

        if(window.link || window.sub_link){
            highlightNav($side_nav)
            highlightNav($side_nav_replace)
        } else {
            var eb_str = getQueryString('eb')
            if(eb_str) {
                var highlightArray = ['top-line', 'quick-news', 'sole', 'special-topic', 'special-column', 'news-retail', 'news-cross', 'news-industry'];
                var is_find = false;
                for (var i = 0; i < highlightArray.length; i += 1) {
                    var reg = new RegExp(highlightArray[i] + '$', 'ig');
                    if (reg.test(eb_str)) {
                        is_find = true;
                        var _str = highlightArray[i];
                        if (/news/g.test(_str)) {
                            var _str_array = highlightArray[i].split('-');
                            window.link = _str_array[0];
                            window.sub_link = _str_array[1];
                        } else {
                            window.link = _str;
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if(!is_find) {
                    window.link = "news"
                }
            } else {
                window.link = "news"
            }

            highlightNav($side_nav)
            highlightNav($side_nav_replace)
        }
     </script>

  <script>
   // 根据JS变量决定是否尝试读取COOKIE里的用户信息身份, 如果没有登录就 继续通过接口获取登录用户信息
        if (window.highConcurrency) {
            //尝试获取COOKIE里的值
            function _getCookie(key) {
                var cookieString = document.cookie;
                var start = cookieString.indexOf(key + "=");
                if (start != -1) {
                    var start = start + key.length + 1;
                    var end = cookieString.indexOf(";", start);
                    if (end == -1) {
                        end = cookieString.length;
                    }
                    return cookieString.substring(start, end);
                }
                return null;
            }

            function getAvatarPath(uid) {
                //返回 高位补0的9位数字的特定格式 '001/52/32/02'
                return ('000000000' + (uid || '')).slice(-9).replace(/(\d{2})(?=(?:\d{2})+$)/g, '$1/');
            }

            var trackUname = decodeURIComponent(_getCookie('trackUname'));
            var trackUid = _getCookie('trackUid');
            if (trackUname && trackUid) {
                //拼装用户信息显示效果
                var my_avatar = 'https://dev.ebrun.com/2009/uc/data/avatar/' + getAvatarPath(trackUid) + '_real_avatar_big.jpg';

                $(".login-panel").append([
                    '<ul class="dropdown-menu user">',
                    '<li>' + trackUname + '</li>',
                    '<li><a rel="nofollow" href="https://u.ebrun.com/user/profile" title="" target="_blank">账号设置</a></li>',
                    '<li><a rel="nofollow" href="https://u.ebrun.com/order/index" title="" target="_blank">订单中心</a></li>',
                    '<li><a rel="nofollow" href="https://u.ebrun.com/user/index" title="" target="_blank">会员中心</a></li>',
                    '<li><a rel="nofollow" href="https://u.ebrun.com/notification/comment" title="" target="_blank">我的消息</a></li>',
                    '<li><a rel="nofollow" href="javascript:void(0);" title="" target="_blank" onclick="window.location.href=\'https://u.ebrun.com/auth/logout?refer=\' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);return false;">退出登录</a></li>',
                    '</ul>',
                    '<a rel="nofollow" href="https://u.ebrun.com/user/index" title="' + trackUname + '" target="_blank">',
                    '<img class="avatar" src="' + my_avatar + '" alt="">',
                    '</a>'].join('')
                );
                window.topbar_global_status_islogin = 1;
            } else {
                $(".login-panel").append('<a rel="nofollow" href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="window.location.href=\'https://u.ebrun.com/auth/login?jump=\' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);return false;">登录</a>');
                window.topbar_global_status_islogin = 0;
            }
        } else {
            var ua = navigator.userAgent;
            if (!new RegExp(ua, 'img').test('spider')) {
                // 为了避免 AJAX + HTTPS 跨域问题, 必须使用 document.write 写入页面
                document.write('<script src="https://www.ebrun.com/index/login?for=2021__topbar"><\/script>');
            } else {
                $(".login-panel").append('<a rel="nofollow" href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="window.location.href=\'https://u.ebrun.com/auth/login?jump=\' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);return false;">登录</a>');
                window.topbar_global_status_islogin = 0;
            }
        }
